				<div id="bodyContent" class="vector-body" aria-labelledby="firstHeading" data-mw-ve-target-container>
					<div class="vector-body-before-content">
							<div class="mw-indicators">
		<div id="mw-indicator-coordinates" class="mw-indicator"><div class="mw-parser-output"><span id="coordinates"><a href="/wiki/Geographic_coordinate_system" title="Geographic coordinate system">Coordinates</a>: <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1156832818">.mw-parser-output .geo-default,.mw-parser-output .geo-dms,.mw-parser-output .geo-dec{display:inline}.mw-parser-output .geo-nondefault,.mw-parser-output .geo-multi-punct,.mw-parser-output .geo-inline-hidden{display:none}.mw-parser-output .longitude,.mw-parser-output .latitude{white-space:nowrap}</style><span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion"><a class="external text" href="https://geohack.toolforge.org/geohack.php?pagename=List_of_Major_League_Soccer_stadiums&amp;params=32_47_04.0_N_117_7_22.2_W_type:landmark_scale:2000"><span class="geo-default"><span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location"><span class="latitude">32°47′04.0″N</span> <span class="longitude">117°7′22.2″W</span></span></span><span class="geo-multi-punct">&#xfeff; / &#xfeff;</span><span class="geo-nondefault"><span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">32.784444°N 117.122833°W</span><span style="display:none">&#xfeff; / <span class="geo">32.784444; -117.122833</span></span></span></a></span></span></div></div>
		</div>

						<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
					</div>
					<div id="contentSub"><div id="mw-content-subtitle"></div></div>
					
					
					<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content"><div class="mw-content-ltr mw-parser-output" lang="en" dir="ltr"><p>


<a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a> (MLS) is the premier professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">soccer</a> league in the United States and Canada. The league has 30 teams in 30 stadiums as of the 2025 season: 27 in the United States and 3 in Canada. At the time of the league's inauguration in 1996, MLS teams used <a href="/wiki/Multi-purpose_stadium" title="Multi-purpose stadium">multi-purpose stadiums</a>, often shared with <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> (NFL) or <a href="/wiki/College_football" title="College football">college football</a> teams. Because of lower attendance, these stadiums had rows of seats covered in tarps to limit capacity. Starting in 1999 with the Columbus Crew's construction of <a href="/wiki/Historic_Crew_Stadium" title="Historic Crew Stadium">Historic Crew Stadium</a>, the league has constructed <a href="/wiki/Soccer-specific_stadium" title="Soccer-specific stadium">soccer-specific stadiums</a> which are tailor-made for soccer and which have smaller capacity. As of 2025<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_Major_League_Soccer_stadiums&amp;action=edit">&#91;update&#93;</a></sup>, 22 of 30 MLS stadiums are soccer-specific stadiums, which generally have a capacity of 18,000 to 30,000 seats.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> While the league's early stadiums relied heavily on public financing, several modern soccer-specific stadiums have been majority-funded by clubs and their owners.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The league's soccer-specific stadiums, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/Providence_Park" title="Providence Park">Providence Park</a> in <a href="/wiki/Portland,_Oregon" title="Portland, Oregon">Portland, Oregon</a>, have grass playing surfaces. The remaining stadiums with <a href="/wiki/Artificial_turf" title="Artificial turf">artificial turf</a> surfaces are mostly used by teams sharing their venues with other sports, including American football.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Pitch sizes range from a width of 70 yards (64&#160;m) used by <a href="/wiki/New_York_City_FC" title="New York City FC">New York City FC</a> at <a href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium" title="Yankee Stadium">Yankee Stadium</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Houston_Dynamo" class="mw-redirect" title="Houston Dynamo">Houston Dynamo</a> at <a href="/wiki/Shell_Energy_Stadium" title="Shell Energy Stadium">Shell Energy Stadium</a>, to 80 yards (73&#160;m) used by the <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">LA Galaxy</a> at <a href="/wiki/Dignity_Health_Sports_Park" title="Dignity Health Sports Park">Dignity Health Sports Park</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>As with the other <a href="/wiki/Major_professional_sports_leagues_in_the_United_States_and_Canada" title="Major professional sports leagues in the United States and Canada">major North American sports leagues</a>, the majority of MLS stadiums have sold their <a href="/wiki/Naming_rights" title="Naming rights">naming rights</a> to corporations. <a href="/wiki/BC_Place" title="BC Place">BC Place</a>, <a href="/wiki/Soldier_Field" title="Soldier Field">Soldier Field</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium" title="Yankee Stadium">Yankee Stadium</a> are the only current MLS stadiums without a corporate-sponsored name. 
</p>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1291884410">.mw-parser-output .locmap .od{position:absolute}.mw-parser-output .locmap .id{position:absolute;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .locmap .pv>div{display:inline;padding:1px}.mw-parser-output .locmap .pl>div{display:inline;padding:1px;float:right}.mw-parser-output .locmap .pr>div{display:inline;padding:1px;float:left}@media (prefers-color-scheme:dark){html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .locmap img{filter:grayscale(0.6)}html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .od,html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .pr>div{background:white!important;color:#000!important}html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .infobox-full-data .locmap div{background:transparent!important}}</style><div class="locmap <div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Future_stadiums">Future stadiums</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Major_League_Soccer_stadiums&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Future stadiums"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The following is a table of future MLS stadiums that are undergoing construction, have been approved for construction, or are existing venues that are planned to be used by a future team.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/New_England_Revolution" title="New England Revolution">New England Revolution</a> have reportedly been in negotiations over a potential site in <a href="/wiki/Everett,_Massachusetts" title="Everett, Massachusetts">Everett, Massachusetts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>42<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Vancouver_Whitecaps_FC" title="Vancouver Whitecaps FC">Vancouver Whitecaps FC</a> are exploring the possibility of building new stadium at the <a href="/wiki/Hastings_Park" title="Hastings Park">Pacific National Exhibition Fairgrounds</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>43<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
